</a></div></nav></div></div></nav><div class="grid-flex-at-medium"><div class="column expand align-center align-left-at-medium"><p class="copyright">© 2021 Square, Inc.</p></div><div class="column align-center align-right-at-medium"><nav><ul class="destination-links reset grid-space-base"><li class="toggle-one-trust-prefs hidden"><a href="#">Cookie Preferences</a></li><li><a href="/us/en/legal/general/privacy">Privacy Notice</a></li><li><a href="/us/en/legal/general/california-privacy">Additional California Privacy Disclosure</a></li><li><a href="/us/en/legal/general/ua">Terms of Service</a></li><li><a href="/us/en/legal/general/licenses">Licenses</a></li><li><a href="/us/en/legal/general/gov">Government</a></li><li><a href="/us/en/legal/capital/capital">Square Capital, LLC</a></li></ul></nav></div></div></div></footer><div class="video-player"><div class="video-player-content"></div><a class="video-close-button" href="#" title="Close"></a></div><script src="https://xms-production-f.squarecdn.com/xms/assets/application-65f8903714451473f549ea2b4a8dcfe14d568734d39d02142e732a0096e946f1.js" nonce="0s5EeloPoacatiWkD1O4SFkiLqVvE2SHlCTKmkkCQ8E="></script><script src="https://xms-production-f.squarecdn.com/xms/assets/precompile/sections/scroll_linked_animation_section-dc4f8fc4f64e068dfa560921138d2c956d21a13576c1638e1d3c1a77fb866e65.js" nonce="0s5EeloPoacatiWkD1O4SFkiLqVvE2SHlCTKmkkCQ8E="></script><script nonce="0s5EeloPoacatiWkD1O4SFkiLqVvE2SHlCTKmkkCQ8E=">(function() {
  const SELECTORS = {
    HEADLINE_TEXT: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero h1',
    HEADER_BUTTON: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero .button',
    HEADER_PICTURE: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero picture',
    HEADER_IMAGE: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero img',
    ANIMATION_SECTION: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero',
    IMAGE_BREAKS: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero .scroll-item[data-content-type="screenshotSection"]',
    IMAGE_BREAK_FROM_QUERY_PARAM: value =>
      `.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero .scroll-item[data-content-type="screenshotSection"].sq-custom-image-break-hero-${value}-container`,
    IMAGE_BREAK_SECTION: '.section-screenshot',
    HEADLINE_FIRST_PART: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero h1 > .sq-custom-split-p-1 > *',
    HEADLINE_SECOND_PART: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero h1 > .sq-custom-split-p-2 > *',
    HEADLINE_FIRST_GROUP:
      '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero h1 > .sq-custom-split-p-1 > *, .sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero h1 > .sq-custom-split-p-2 > *',
    HEADLINE_NEXT_GROUP: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero h1 > .sq-custom-split-p-3',
    EXIT_WAYPOINT: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero-exit-waypoint',
    SHOW_RANDOM_IMAGE: '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero--show-random',
  };

  const imageBreakPattern = /sq-custom-image-break-hero-(.*)+-container/;

  const addWaypoints = () => {
    // add waypoints
    // do immediately and not wait till ready or load
    $('<div class="sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero-exit-waypoint"></div>').appendTo(
      '.sq-custom-2021-q1-brand-campaign-hero',
    );
  };

  const trackSelectedImage = ({ selectedImageBreak, showSpecific }) => {
    const imageLabelMatch = selectedImageBreak.classList.value.match(imageBreakPattern);

    const category = 'Hero Image';
    const action = 'View';
    const feature = 'Brand Campaign Hero Image';
    const properties = {
      entry_id: selectedImageBreak.dataset.entryId,
      hero_image_label: imageLabelMatch && imageLabelMatch[1],
      from_query_param: showSpecific,
      feature,
    };

    //  ES
    Sq.Tracking.trackEvent(
      category,
      action,
      properties, // or event label
      1, // event value
      true, // nonInteraction - true tells GA to ignore event in bounce-rate calculation
    );

    if (Sq.Tracking.useCDP) {
      // CDP
      Sq.Tracking.filterCDPProperties(properties);
      Sq.Tracking.cdp.track(`${action} ${category}`, properties);
    }
  };

  const pickImage = () => {
    // select one image
    const allImageBreaks = $(SELECTORS.IMAGE_BREAKS);
    const SHOWN_IMAGES_SELECTORS = `shownImagesSelectors-${window.location.pathname}`;
    const QUERY_PARAM_KEY = 'sq-campaign-seller';
    const urlParams = Sq.UrlState.getUrlParams();
    const showSpecific = QUERY_PARAM_KEY in urlParams;
    let showRandom = !showSpecific;

    let selectedImageBreak;
    let subsetImageBreaks;

    if (allImageBreaks.length > 1) {
      if (showSpecific) {
        // URL query param based image
        const imageBreakFromQueryParam = $(SELECTORS.IMAGE_BREAK_FROM_QUERY_PARAM(urlParams[QUERY_PARAM_KEY]));
        if (allImageBreaks.is(imageBreakFromQueryParam)) {
          selectedImageBreak = imageBreakFromQueryParam.get(0);
        } else {
          showRandom = true;
        }
      }

      if (showRandom) {
        const showRandomEnabled = $(SELECTORS.SHOW_RANDOM_IMAGE).length > 0;
        if (showRandomEnabled) {
          let alreadyShownSelectors = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem(SHOWN_IMAGES_SELECTORS)) || [];
          if (alreadyShownSelectors.length >= allImageBreaks.length) {
            subsetImageBreaks = allImageBreaks;
            alreadyShownSelectors = [];
          } else {
            subsetImageBreaks = allImageBreaks.not($(alreadyShownSelectors));
          }
          selectedImageBreak = subsetImageBreaks.get(Math.floor(Math.random() * subsetImageBreaks.length));
          alreadyShownSelectors.push(
            Array.from(selectedImageBreak.classList)
              .map(s => `.${s}`)
              .join(''),
          );
          sessionStorage.setItem(SHOWN_IMAGES_SELECTORS, JSON.stringify(alreadyShownSelectors));
        } else {
          // pick the first one
          selectedImageBreak = allImageBreaks.get(0);
        }
      }

      allImageBreaks.not(selectedImageBreak).remove();
    } else {
      selectedImageBreak = allImageBreaks.get(0);
    }

    $(function() {
      // wait for Sq.Tracking to load and init
      trackSelectedImage({ selectedImageBreak, showSpecific });
    });

    return selectedImageBreak;
  };

  const setupAnimation = selectedImageBreak => {
    $.extend(Sq.ScrollLinkedAnimationConfig, {
      '2021-q1-brand-campaign-header-medium': {
        scenes: [
          {
            name: 'header-exit',
            options: {
              duration: '150%',
              triggerHook: 0.5,
              triggerElement: SELECTORS.EXIT_WAYPOINT,
            },
            playOnScroll: true,
            timeline: {
              parameters: {
                autoplay: false,
                easing: 'easeOutQuad',
              },
              animations: [
                {
                  parameters: {
                    targets: [SELECTORS.HEADER_IMAGE],
                    perspective: ['1000px', '1000px'],
                    translateX: ['-50%', '-50%'],
                    // translateY: ['0px', '-100px'],
                    translateZ: ['0px', '20px'],
                    rotateX: ['0deg', '5deg'],
                    rotateZ: [0, 0],
                    duration: 400,
                    easing: 'linear',
                  },
                },
                {
                  parameters: {
                    targets: [SELECTORS.HEADLINE_FIRST_PART],
                    translateX: ['0px', '-10px'],
                    translateZ: [0, 0],
                    duration: 800,
                  },
                  offset: '-=400',
                },
                {
                  parameters: {
                    targets: [SELECTORS.HEADLINE_SECOND_PART],
                    translateX: ['0px', '10px'],
                    translateZ: [0, 0],
                    duration: 800,
                  },
                  offset: '-=800',
                },
                {
                  parameters: {
                    targets: [SELECTORS.HEADLINE_TEXT, SELECTORS.HEADER_BUTTON],
                    perspective: ['1000px', '1000px'],
                    translateZ: ['0px', '20px'],
                    rotateX: ['0deg', '-5deg'],
                    rotateZ: [0, 0],
                    duration: 800,
                  },
                  offset: '-=800',
                },
              ],
            },
          },
        ],
      },
    });

    const onLoadAnimationTimeline = {
      parameters: {
        autoplay: true,
        easing: 'easeOutQuad',
      },
      animations: [
        {
          parameters: {
            targets: SELECTORS.HEADLINE_FIRST_GROUP,
            opacity: {
              value: [0, 1],
              easing: 'easeOutSine',
            },
            translateY: ['30px', '0px'],
            translateZ: [0, 0],
            duration: 800,
            delay: anime.stagger(50, { easing: 'linear' }),
          },
        },
        {
          parameters: {
            targets: [SELECTORS.HEADLINE_NEXT_GROUP, SELECTORS.HEADER_BUTTON],
            opacity: {
              value: [0, 1],
              easing: 'easeOutSine',
            },
            translateY: ['30px', '0px'],
            translateZ: [0, 0],
            duration: 800,
            delay: anime.stagger(50, { easing: 'easeOutSine' }),
          },
          offset: '-=800',
        },
      ],
    };

    // on image load
    $(function() {
      $(selectedImageBreak)
        .find('img')
        .on('load', function() {
          const scrollLinkedAnimation = $(SELECTORS.ANIMATION_SECTION)
            .data(Sq.ScrollLinkedAnimationSection.DATA_KEY);
          scrollLinkedAnimation.initAnimeTimeline(onLoadAnimationTimeline);
          // animeTimeline.play();

          // add image loaded class
          $(selectedImageBreak)
            .find(SELECTORS.IMAGE_BREAK_SECTION)
            .attr('data-image-loaded', true);
        })
        .each(function() {
          if (this.complete) {
            $(this).trigger('load'); // For jQuery >= 3.0
          }
        });
    });
  };

  addWaypoints();
  const selectedImageBreak = pickImage();
  setupAnimation(selectedImageBreak);
})();
</script></body></html>
